4a2(rgyud): yang na bcom ldan 'das mthong bar 'tshal nas/ rang nyid kyis gsol cig
4a3(rgyud): rjod la/ rang gis blang bar bya'o// de nas skad cig dngos grub mchog yid

7a1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul du sems dpa' chen po brgyad bri bar bya'o// de nas zla ba nya nas brtsams te/ phyag rgya chen por brtsams la/ de bzhin du sngon du bsnyen pa'i tshul lhar bzlas
7a2(rgyud): nas zla ba nya'i mtshan mo thog thag tu/ ci lta ba bzhin du sko bar ma gyur pas/ phyag rgya ma dkrol bar bzlas brjod pa'o// de nas nang par bcom ldan 'das kyi zhal 'dzum zhing / zla ba dang mnyam pa'i mdangs
7a3(rgyud): can mthong bar rtsol cing / sangs rgyas nyid dang rje rje 'dzin pa nyid la sogs pa'i dngos grub mchog rnams rtsol bar 'gyur ro// cho ga gzhar yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa/ byang chub sems dang / 
7a4(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po brgyad kyis yongs su skor ba dang / phyogs du de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang / rdo rje 'chang thams cad bri bar bya'o// de nas de bzhin du bsgrubs pas sangs rgyas nyid la sog
7a5(rgyud): pa dngos grub thams cad 'grub po// ras la bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje snyems pa dang bcas pa bris la/ de'i sman sngar dang po phyag rgya chen pos gnas nas bzlas brjod 'bum byas nas/ 'bum rdzogs nas phyag
7a6(rgyud): na rdo rje nyid thob par 'gyuraro// de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dpa'o gcig pa bris nas/ de bzhin du mthar sangs rgyas par 'gyu ro// de nas klags pa tsam gyis 'grub pa'i las rnams dkyil 'khor du zhugs pa
7a7(rgyud): tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur ba ni/ 'di ltar ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rje su mnyes par bya ba la ni/ 'dod chags la sogs pa'i dbang po thams cad dul bas so// rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po mnyes par bya ba
7a8(rgyud): la ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' dang 'khrud cing 'od byed pas so// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mnyes par bya ba la ni/ dpag tu med pa'i bzlas pas so// rdo rje thams cad mnyes par bya ba la ni/ rang gi snying po bcwa
7b1(rgyud): pas so// lhal sogs pa'i sems can rjes su chags par bya ba la ni/ thams cad du 'bum bzlas pas so// bdag bsrung ba la ni yungs kar dang lan gcig gis so// gzhan ba srung ba la ni rdo rje zhe sa
7b2(rgyud): thams cad bsrung ba la ni yid kyis lan gcig go// mtshams dang phyogs dang dkyil 'khor thams cad bcing ba la ni lta ba 'am yungs kar la sogs pas so// sems can rengs pas byed pa la ni
7b3(rgyud): dbugs mi 'byid par bzlas pas so// sems cad thams cad rdugs par bya ba la ni/ rdo rje bcing bas so// sems can thams cad rmongs par byed pa la ni/ mig btsums nas bzlas pas so// thams
7b4(rgyud): cad bsad pa la ni rdo rje bral bas so// sems can thams cad rgyas btab pa la ni/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i rgya phyag rgyas so// tham cad snying 'dren cing 'byin pa la ni/ yid kyis bzlas paso
7b5(rgyud): sems can thams cad skrag par bya ba la ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/ kyi phyag rgyas so// nor thams cad dgug pa la ni gser gyi zlas paso nor dang 'bru thams cad dgug pa la ni rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i
7b6(rgyud): phyag rgyas so// thams cad rjesu chags pa la ni/ pi wang gdung ba dang bcas pa'i ka ka'i gru len pas bzlas brjod pa'o// thams cad 'bigs pa dang / de rjerje su chags par bya ba la ni/ rdo rje mda'i phyag rgyab
7b7(rgyud): thams cad dga' bar bya ba la ni phyogs thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes paso// bsdug pa'i mche bstan par bya ba la ni/ snying pos mnyes par mchi rabs so// ma rungs pa sgrub pa la ni rdo rje snyems paso
7b8(rgyud): brgyan thams cad 'phrog pa la ni/ 'bar ba'i lta bas 'phrog pas so// thams cad yid tshim pa la ni rdo rje khu tshur sIng khar gzhag pas so// mun pas snang ba la ni rdo rje kha sha re da ltas te skor bas so// lus
9a1(rgyud): tshig rtagacad g.yog par bya ba la ni/ zhi ba'i gnas su 'dum smras pas so// thams cad la lan ldon pa la ni/ rde dzumadzad kyi dngos so// rdzu 'phrul dang thams cad bstan pa la ni rdi rje rdzu 'phrul bye byag rgyas so// 
9a2(rgyud): Tham/ byang 'phrul thams cad bstan pa la ni rdo rje ting nge 'dzin gyi mchog gis so// rang gi lus la sogs pa'i dngos po thams cad la sangs rgyas dang / rdo rje sems dpa' la sogs pa sku dang mi sruba'i dngos po thams cad sam
9a3(rgyud): pa la ni/ rdo rje rnam par 'phrul pas so// lha thams cad dba' pa la ni rdo rje skor bas so// klu thams cad rje su 'brangs pa la ni klu'i rgyal po'i mtshor bzlas brjod pa'o// gnod sbyin thams cad mngag gzhug byas pa/ 
9a4(rgyud): la ni/ rdo rje bka' sgobs so// 'byung po thams cad 'dul ba ni da lha chen po mnan nas khros pas zlas brjod bya'o// serab thams cad bzlog pa la ni// rdo rje bsrung gi phyag rgyas so// klog 'bab pa
9a5(rgyud): thams cad bzlog pa ni/ rdo rje khro gnyer can gyi phyag rgyas so// cha dbab pa la ni klu'i mtshor bzlas brjod pa'o// char bcad pa la ni drim med pa chu sbyin bya'o// smin bskyed pa la ni/ klu bris nas gdugs
9a6(rgyud): pas bdug par bya'o// sprin gshig pa la ni rdo rje namakha'i sprin gyis so// chu med pa'i phyogasu shin du bsil ba'i tshe'i phyogs rtag tu 'byung ba la ni rdo rje klu'i phyag rgyas so// gter thams cad shes par bya ba la ni c+doM
9a7(rgyud): du chu thugs par bya'o// gtar thams cad dgog ba la ni rdo rje 'byor gyis so// gter thams cad rnyed pa lnga ni rdo rje nor skyes so// rgyal srid thams cad thob par bya ba la rdo rjod bang skur ba'i tshogs so// sa'-i bdag por/ 
9a8(rgyud): bya ba la ni rdo rje sems dpa' dbang skur ba'i phyag rgyas so// dkyil 'khor thams cad sgrub pa'i la ni// rdo rje 'khor lo phyag rgyas so// phyag rgya thams cad sgrub pa la ni// bde ba chen po'i dam
9b1(rgyud): tshig gi phyag rgyas so// dam tshig thams cad sgrub pa la ni/ rab tu dga' ba'i rdo rje'i phyag rgyas so// dngos po sgrub pa lan rdo snyems pa'i ljags kyu'i phyag rgyas so// ma grub pa thams cad
9b2(rgyud): grub pa lon rdo rje sgrub pa'i phyag rgyas so// rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad la ni// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin pa'i phyag rgyas so// rdo rje thams cad sgrub pa la ni// rdo rje thams cad kyi mchog gis so phyag rgyas so// 
9b3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad sgrub pa li ni/ thugs kyi rdo rjes so// rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid sgrub pa la ni/ rdo rje sems dpa'i phyag rgyas so// sangs rgyas nyid sgrub pa la ni// rdo rje ye shes kyi phyag rgyas so// 
9b4(rgyud): bode ba chen po'i don yod pa'i dam tshig chen po de kho na nyid rdo rje zhes bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzog s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ yang de
9b5(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis zhi ba'i chos nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub sgrub pa zhes bya ba'i/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul du 'di gsungs te// rdo rje bsra ba nyid kyi phyir
9b6(rgyud): rdo rje mnyam pa nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa ni/ byang chub chen po'o// don cig pa nyid kyi phyir mnyam pa nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa la ni/ byang chub chen po'o// ngo bo nyid rnam par dag pa
9b7(rgyud): phyir chos kyi mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa ni/ byang chub chen po'o// thams cad la rnam par mi rtog pa nyid kyi phyir mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa ni/ byang chub chen po'o// ngo bo nyid lag na rdo rje gang la la chos
9b8(rgyud): mngon par sgrub bzhi po// 'di dag nyan pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang / sgom pa de sdig pa thams cad las smod kyang bad chab snying po la thug gi bar du ngan song thams cad las yang dag par 'das par
10a1(rgyud): ma pa mi nga 'dig su sa/ sa dres su mas kyi de ga gas pa nga sa dgung dus par mdza com lda ma
10a2(rgyud): bzhugs pa dag rnams dpa nib brgyad 'i dkyil labyor du thugs pabyo drong du sa/ de mya bcom lda sa nin ga cigs pa ma par bye sa na ga shems pa blangs ca kyi
10a3(rgyud): dkyil 'khor byi gyis rlob pa zhes bya 'i/ nga 'dzi la stsob ba nugs ras/ dri ba zhi gshegs pa rnams cad kyi ngo khon nyid rde rje zhes bya ba'i de chag rkyen po'i shul mkhor chen po 'di gsungs so// 
10a4(rgyud): rdo rje sems dnga'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i dul du bya'id kyi kyiladzin rjes la/ de'i lus su rtsig gsu gyis 'khor lo bris la bcom ldan 'das kyi thad dkar sa tshogs pa ma rab tu gnas pa
10a5(rgyud): de'i 'khor lo'i lte ba la/ bcom ldar 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rtag pa chen po'o// sal sogs pa las bang gnag po ngo'o// nga'i phyogs thams cad dus la so gas pa las byas pa'i dponi da ga shegs pa
10a6(rgyud): brkyang gzhag gas bri bar bya'o// de nas mtshon gyi thig le rnams kyis dkyil 'khor la ba zhugs pa'i de bzhi go shegs pa rnams rdo rje 'dzin pa dang 'anasu pa bri dang bya'o// phyi'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyogs pa ni 'tsha
10a7(rgyud): rnamasu byang chub sems dpa'o brgyad ji lta ba bzhin du gzhag la/ bum pa rkang ba bzhi sgo rnams su dgod par bya zhing / byang chub kyi mtshan mo rnams gzhag par bya ste/ shar nas brtsams te/ ne'us gang bya
10b1(rgyud): dang bcas pa'i bu dang / ro drug gis bkang zhing dbyig dang gse dung de'i rlo bo che dang gos la sogs pas yongs su gang ba'i snod dang 'jom zhing shin du bde ba'i stan dang sangs rgyas kyi sku gzugs dgos / 
10b2(rgyud): de nas de bzhin du gos gyon la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i phyag rgya bcings la zhugs nas/ bdag nyid slob dpon med par yi bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis
10b3(rgyud): rlob par 'gyur ba/ nga bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rtog pa dang / dngas grub thams cad la mi tshugs pa drus sa gsod pa dang / sgrib pa byams cad dang dril 'a thob par 'gyur ro// de nas slob mo yong ga nun
10b4(rgyud): zhugs nas rdo rje rtse lnga pa byin la rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur bu yang byin gyis bya'o// de nas dam tshig 'di dag bgo par bya'o// sems can kun la phani phyi dang // brtan pa thams cad grub pa'i
10b5(rgyud): rnam par mi rtog sbyor ba yis// ci bde bar ni thams cad gyis kyi zhes brjid do// de nas mtshan ma bzhi'i smor ba so ji lta bso ska d+hi lta ba bzhin sbyin par byo'o// d+ham gyi mad po'i dkyil 'khrutshar
10b6(rgyud): de nas bsgrub pa ni ras la bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad 'dzum pa dang bcas pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur gyi phyag rgya yongasu 'dzin par bya'o// gzhan thams cad dam tshig chen
10b7(rgyud): dkyil 'khor du tshul du bya'o// de nas de bzhin du sems dpa' mchog bsgrub pa dag dngos grub mchog rnams kyang de bzhin no// gzhan yang ngas la bcom ldan 'dus dpa' bo gcig bre bris te/ de'i mdun
10b8(rgyud): du rdo rje tshig gis bzlas brjod 'bum byas na/ ye shes kyi khu tshur yongasu 'dzin pas mtshan mo theg thag bzlas na/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa thob cing / dngos grub thams cad 'grub pa'i byang chub sa
11a1(rgyud): debar 'gyur la de nas de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur// de nas ma bsgrubs pas kyang dkyil 'khor du zhugs pa cas nyid kyis las rnams 'grub par 'gyur ro// 'di lta ste de bzhin gshegs pa thaman
11a2(rgyud): cad la mchod pa la ni ji snyed pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba thams cad bul bas so// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mchod pa la ni/ bdag phul bas so/ dkon mchog mchod pa la ni
11a3(rgyud): me tog bzlas pas so// sems can thams cad mchod pa la ni thams cad byams pas bzlas pas so// chos thams cad bsdud pa la ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshig bzhi po 'don pas so// bdud
11a4(rgyud): thams cad 'dul ba la ni gtan zhing nges pa'i bzlas pas so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i/ thob pa la ni rgyan thams cad phul zhing rang nyid bcings pas so// de
11a5(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba thob pa chos nyid thaMd thob pa la ni/ rdo rje pad ma la ni lta bas so// de bzhin gsheg pa thams cad kyi las kyi dngos grub thob pa la ni thams cad rdo rje'i las
11a6(rgyud): kyi mchog gis so// sangs rgyas nyid rab tu thob pa la ni/ rdo rje ye shes phyag rgya chen pos so// bde ba thams cad don yod pa'i dam tshig rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de/ 
11a7(rgyud): na nyid kyi rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// // de nas ma rungs pa thams cad 'dul ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas yang chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyis rnam
11a8(rgyud): par rgyal ba bsdus pa zhes bya'o// shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa bsgrub pa 'di gsungs so// 'dod chags kyi spros pa med pa nyid kyis zhe sdang gi spros pa med pa nyid do// zhe sdang gi spros pa med pa nyid kyis gti
11b1(rgyud): mug gi spros pa med pa nyid do// chos thams cad spros pa med pa nyid kyis shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa spros pa med pa nyid do// rig par bya'o// lag na rdo rje gang la la shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di nyan pa dang / 
11b2(rgyud): 'dzin pa dang / sgom pa des 'dul ba'i dbang gis phyir khams gsum du skyes pa'i sems can thams cad bsad kyang ngan song du skye bar mi 'gyur te/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon
11b3(rgyud): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par 'gyuraro// de nas bcom ldan 'das la rdo rje chos nyid 'di'i don rgya cher ston cing 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya bcings nas khro gnyer dang bcas shing
11b4(rgyud): smin ma bteg te/ 'bar bar lta ba la pad ma'i gdong khro zhing bkod de/ mche brtsigs nas rkang pa g.yas pa'i bskum pa'i tshul du gnas pas gnas nas/ rdo rje hU~M zhes bya ba'i snying po 'di gsungs so// hUM/ de nas/ 
11b5(rgyud): 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi 'dod pa'i dang // phyug la sogs pa'i 'jig rten gsum gyi bdag po rnams da la yang dag par bkug ste/ ltung bar mdzad nas/ dkyil 'khor du
11b6(rgyud): bcug nas rnam par rgyal ba mdzad la bcings te/ dbang du byas shI 'dul zhing / rje su btul te/ blangs nas yang dam tshig gi bcings nas 'jig rten gyi bdag po dbang phyug chen po'i chung ma dang
11b7(rgyud): bcas pa/ zhabs gnyisu phub nas/ mnan par mdzad do// de nas de rnams kyis 'jig rten gsum po thams cad du sgra chen po bsgrags te/ kye rdo rje 'chang yongasu bskyab par mdzad cig/ bdag pa ga phab rnams ma
11b8(rgyud): gzir cig/ 'dir khyod la bdag skyabasu mchi'o// dam tshig dang sgo ba yang dag par sgrub par bgyi'o// ma mo thams cad 'dul zhing ka la btags nas dkyil 'khor yang rnam par bshig ste/ phyag rgya tha~Md dang / 
12a1(rgyud): dam tshig kyang bral zhing / rnam par gshig pa dang / gdon thams cad kyang bzlog cing / nad thams cad dang rims tha dang gnod pa dang / dug dang ngan 'gro rnams bral zhing rnam pa ru ga shig/ sgra chen po sgrag
12a2(rgyud): shing 'jigs pa chen pos 'jigs par byed pa'i tshig nyid kyis bcom ldan 'das nyid la skyabs song ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang zhal rnam par gzhang rnam nas/ de rnams dkyil 'khor du bcug te/ dam tshig gis bcing
12a3(rgyud): nas rdo rje rin chen gyis dbang skur nas/ rang gi mtshan pa rnams la rdo rje byin gyis brlabs te/ rdo rje ming gis dbang sgyur ba yang rjesu btsal nas/ sems can ma lus pa'i don du phyi rdo rje'i rigasuM rab tu gzhag go/ de nas
12a4(rgyud): rdo rje khro bo'i rdo rje las/ phyag na rdo rje dang 'dra ba'i dngos po bdag nyid can kha dog dang / brgyan dang mtshon cha rnam pa sna tshogs pa bsnams pa rnam par 'gyur ba'i rdo rje'i rigs su mtsho ba brtsigs pata/ tshems kyis
12a5(rgyud): sgros mnon pa/ smin ma mi zad cing / khro gnyer gnyer ba/ spyan dang dbu skra dang ag com 'bar ba/ zhal 'jigs pa/ 1/ rdo rje dang lcags kyu dang / zhags pa dang mtshan cha mda' dang / dbyig
12a6(rgyud): pa kha tra~M kha dang / gri rings dang / chu gri phyag na bsnams pa/ khro bo chen po hUM mdzad las phyung ste/ bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis bzhugs so// lha la sogs pa do
12a7(rgyud): rnams kyang rang gi dkyil 'khor gyis byin gyis brlabs nas/ phyi'i dkyil 'khor de gzhag go// gdon la sogs pa de dag kyang dkyil 'khor gyi phyi rim na gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
12a8(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad thugs rje chen po'i thabs khro bo'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhags so// khams gsum mtha' dag las rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba rdo rje byin gyis brlabs pa 'di
12b1(rgyud): gsung so// de nas yang dag bshad bya ba// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ste/ khams gsum rnam par rgyal zhes pa// 'dul ba chen po 'dul byed pa// dkyil 'khor dang po sbyor ba yis// phyi'i dkyil
12b2(rgyud): 'khor dang po sbyor ba yis// phyi'i dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// de yi nang gi dkyil 'khor brgyad pa dag dang mtshungs// de yi dbus su khro bo che// phyag na rdo rje gzhag par bya// sangs rgyas phreng la stsogs
12b3(rgyud): pas smras// ud dpal sngon po'i 'dab 'dra ba// zhol ni cung zad mche ba rtsigs// khro bcas gzhad pa'i zhal mnga' ba// g.yon rkyang ba yaus legs bzhugs lo// rdo rje hUM mdzad bsdus pas
12b4(rgyud): g.yon gyi zhabs kyis legs gnas pa// de yi dbang phyug che// g.yas kyi dka' thub zlog pa yi// nu ma'i skyengasurnga rab tu 'jog/ 'bar phrer 'jigs pa'i 'od ldan pa// sa g.yogs
12b5(rgyud): bcas pa'i khams rnams kyi/ khro bo kun du gzhag par bya// / 'bar phreng 'khrigs pa'i 'od ldan pa'i// 'khor/ rtsel de yang gzhag par bya/ 'brar ba 'khrigs pa'i 'od can bri/ 
12b6(rgyud): phyi'i dkyil 'khor gnas rnams// phyi yi dkyil 'khor tshogs rnams so// khro bo'i mtshan ma bzhi po ni// gzhu dang mda' dang / ral gri dang // 'khor lo de bzhin rtse gas sbreng // sgo rnams kun
12b7(rgyud): du bri bar bya// phyi rol gnas pa'i don rnams kyis// sna tshogs gtor mas bkang ba dang / ba dun sngon pos dril btags shing // rtse mo kho dog sna tshogs pa'o// de nas 'jug pa la ni yan lag thams ca
12b8(rgyud): res sngon po zung gis g.yogs shing // khros pas rdo rje dam tshig gi phyag rgya dang bcas pas 'dzin pa zhugs na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis rdo rje'i rigs kyi slob dpon du byin gyis brlabs nas mdzad do// 
13a1(rgyud): dengs partsa mas te sdig pa la sogs pa rnam par grol zhing mi bsod pa dang mi tshugs pa dab mu stegs thams cad car bcad pa dang / phan thogs nus shing thams cad las rgyal ba dang ngos
13a2(rgyud): grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas slob ma de bzhin du bcug la/ snying po byin te dkyil 'khor thams cad du bya'o// de nas rdo rje rnon pa rtsobs bzhi 'bar ba byin la/ rdo rje ming gis dpar skur bas dbang skur
13a3(rgyud): la/ rdo rje rdul shugs byin par byas te// 'di ni bdug pa 'dul byed pa/ lag na rdo rje rdo rje ste// ma rungs thams cad 'dul ba la// khyod kyis kyang ni rtag tu bcang // de nas de bzhin du 'byung bar bya'o// rdo rje'i dkyil
13a4(rgyud): 'khor ro// de nas sgrub pa la ni ras la bcom ldan 'das khro dpo dbang phyug byas la/ rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi tshogs kyang sems dpa' chen po thams cad bya'o// phyogs thams cad du ni lha la sogs pa/ 
13a5(rgyud): dang / ma mo rnams bro bar bya ste/ de nas grub pa thams cad la yang de bzhin te/ de bzhin du dngos grub mchog rnams la ni/ ras la bcom ldan 'das ji lta ba bzhin byas nas/ de'i mdun du lag
13a6(rgyud): pa gnyis kyis phyag rgya bcings te zlas brjod 'bum bya'o// de nas yige hUM tsam gyis 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i las thams cad byed par 'gyur ro// ma bsgrungs par yang las rnams thams cad du/ 
13a7(rgyud): de bzhin du thams cad rjes su chags par bya ba dgug pa bya ba dang / gzhug pa dang / bcing ba dang / dkrol ba dang / dbang du bya ba dang / lkugs par bya ba dang / rings par bya ba dang / rmongs pa bya ba
13a8(rgyud): dang gnyid med par bya ba dang / rgyas btab pa dang / ltung ba dang / brdeg pa dang / bsod ba dang / gso ba la sogs po yang lan gcig zlas par byed par 'gyuraro// thams cad gas dpas ni/ rje
13b1(rgyud): khro bo'i mthar byed kyis so// thams cad rgyas btab pa la nI khro bo'i lhas pa'i zlas pas so/ thams cad gzhig pa la ni rdo rje khros pas gzhig par bya'o/ thams cad nges par gnon pa la ni rdo rje dang khros pas
13b2(rgyud): phyogs der brdeg par bya'o// nad thams cad 'bug pa la ni rdo rje phra mo 'bigs byed kyis so// thams cad kyi snying 'byin pa la ni// khros pa'i yid kyis 'byung bar bya'o// 'dug pa thams cad tshar bcad par bya ba la
13b3(rgyud): na/ khros pa'i rdo rje skor bas so// bdug cing khros pas dga' ba la ni/ khros pas lcags che'i sbyin sreg gis so// bdud thams cad brlag pani/ rang gi sa bon gyi sbyin sreg gis so// gdon thams cad skad
13b4(rgyud): pa la ni/ ha ha zhes rgod cing gzhad pas so// klu thams cad mngon pa la ni/ rdo rje la brdebs nas bzlas pas so// lha thams cad lhung bar bya ba la ni/ lha mo rdo rje ltung byed kyis so// lha'i
13b5(rgyud): bdag po thams cad dbang du bya ba dang / gdul ba dang bsnun pa dang / gsad pa dang / gang gdul bar bya ba la ni/ rdo rje srid pa gsum po 'dul bar byed pas so// rnam thos sras rjes su 'brang
13b6(rgyud): bar bya ba la ni rnam thos sros mnan nas/ khros pas bzlas brjod bya'o// lus ngan po mnan nas dpal 'brog pa la ni/ rdo rje skyes bus so// 'dod pa'i lha'i dbang du bya ba la ni/ 'dod pa'i lha'i mdun du khros/ 
13b7(rgyud): pas bzlas brjod bya'o// tshangs pa ltung ba la ni rdo rje rab tu 'bar 'dod pa'i lha dbang du bya ba la ni/ 'dod pa'i lha'i mdun du/ rgya phyag rgyas so// khyab 'jug gzhig pa la ni rdo rje 'khor lo dra bas so// phyag
13b8(rgyud): rgya chen po 'dul ba'i bya ba la ni/ rdo rje tri shul las bral bso/ ma mo thams cad gsang po la ni/ rdo rje khro bo'i tshogs kyi srin mos so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi phyag rgya dang / dam tshig dang chos dang
14a1(rgyud): gsang ba'i dngos grub rnam par gtor zhing / rnam par gshig pa la ni rdo rje khro bo bdug pa'i dam tshig 'jig par byed pas so/ ri dang shing dang khyim dang mug lag khang dang / grong khyer dang
14a2(rgyud): mchod rten dang / lnga'i khang pa dang / skyes pa drung bud med dang / glang po dang bcas pa'i rta la sogs pa thams cad gnom pa la mi rdo rje khro bo'i mig le reg pas so// ltung ba thams cad bslang ba la ni/ rdo rje khro bos
14a3(rgyud): blangs pas so// thams cad spong ba la no/ rdo rje khro bo'i rdu 'byorams so// thams cad brog pa la ni rdo rje khro bo'i khu tshur dang / du brog pas so// 'jigs pa thams cad bskyed pa la ni/ rdo rje rje dza
14a4(rgyud): lta bas so// dpung thams cad bsad pa la ni/ rdo rje khro za'i gnod sbyin mas so// gzhan gyi dpung thams cad gzhom pa dang / gnon/ pa dang / mongs par byed pa dang / long bar bya ba dang / rgyas btab pa dang
14a5(rgyud): gsad pa la ni/ rdo rje khro bo ma rungs pa'i srin mas so// rgyal po la sogs pa'i mi thams cad bsang ba la ni/ dong kha'i shing la ras kyi khrag gos sbyin sreg byas pas so// lha thams cad rnam par gshig pa la ni thang
14a6(rgyud): kyi gzugs brnyan phur bus gdab pas so// lha'i bdag po thams cad sreg pa la ni/ lha thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyi yam gyi shing gis so// rang gi khrag gi rgyun dbab pas/ sa thams cad nub par bya ba la ni
14a7(rgyud): rdo rje khro ba'i sa 'gog gi phyag rgyas so// khams gsum bsal ba la ni/ rdo rje 'jigs pa'i phyag rgyas so// 'jig rten gsum po thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba la ni/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam par
14a8(rgyud): rgyal ba'i mchog gi rdo rje khro bos so/ khams gsum thams cad dbab pa dang dgug pa dang / gzhug pa dang dab dub pa dang/ nges par bya ba gnon pa la ni/ rdo rje sems dpa'i khro bo'i phyag rgyas so// 
14b1(rgyud): khams gsum thams cad rjes su chags par bya ba dang / dgug pa dang gzhug pa dang / bcing ba dang / rgyas gdab pa dang / dbang du bya ba dang / gnod par bya ba dang / sgrub par bya ba la ni/ bde ba chen po rdo rje khro
14b2(rgyud): bos so// bde ba chen po rdo rje chen po rdo rje khro bo'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ngo bo nyid dag pa'i chos nyid
14b3(rgyud): thob pas/ yang chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid spyan res gzigs dbang gi ye shes kyi phyag rgya zhes bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di gsungs te/ 'dod chags thams cad rnam par dag pas/ 
14b4(rgyud): 'jig rten na sems can thams cad rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// dri ma thams cad rnam par dag pas 'jig rten sdig pa thams cad rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// chos thams cad rnam par dag pas 'jig rten na
14b5(rgyud): sems can thams cad rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// shes pa thams cad rnam par dag pas/ 'jig rten na shes rab kyi pha/ rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag go// lag na rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol
14b6(rgyud): tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di nyan pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang / sgom pa de 'dod chags dang / dri ma thams cad kyi nang na 'dug kyang pad mo lta bur 'dod chags kyi nges pa rnams dang / dri ma rnams dang / 
14b7(rgyud): blo bur gyi nyon mongs pa rnams kyis gos par mi 'gyur ro/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
14b8(rgyud): po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug don gyi gnas/ 'di nyid yang rgya cher ston cing / bzhin rab tu 'dzum mul te/ pad mo'i 'od ba ma kha 'byed pas 'dod chags la sogs pa'i dra mas mi gos pa la lta zhing / 'gro
15a1(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi phyir pad ma'i gzugs sna tshogs nas bya ba'i snying po 'di gsungs so// pri de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis pad ma chen po de las de bzhin gshegs pa la sogs pa'i gzugs
15a2(rgyud): thams cad bcom ldan 'das 'drab bad pas mtshanam pa'i gzugs ca dngos par byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi dang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshul du bcugs par gyur to// de nas yang bcom
15a3(rgyud): ldan 'das spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug chos thams cad la gzigs pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ 'gro ba thams cad 'dul ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di gsung so// 
15a4(rgyud): byi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba'i nang bu gnyis pa ni zur ba ni pa la de bzhin du sgo dang 'tshams su bcas pa zla'o// de nas dkyil 'khor brgyang pa'i tshul du theg bzhis thig btub pa la mtshon dam lnga
15a5(rgyud): pad ma 'dab ma brgyad pa bri bar bya'o// de'i dbus su bcom ldan 'das dgod par bya'o// de'i mdun du bcom ldan 'das pad ma chen po chags pa sku mdog dmar po 'dzin pa/ pad ma chen po dang
15a6(rgyud): mnga' dang gzhu bsnams pa/ g.yas su bcom ldan 'das pad ma chen po'i gtum mo'i dbang phyug/ dbang phyug chen po'i gzugs 'dzin pa gzhag go// rgyab du pang mchen po khyab 'jug gi gzugs 'dzin pa sku mdog
15a7(rgyud): nag por 'dug par bya'o// g.yon du pad ma chen po mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pa'i gzugs 'dzin pa/ sku mdog dkar por gzhag par bya'o// g.yas kyi 'tshams su pang ma chen po dkar po sa 'dzin pa gzhag
15a8(rgyud): par bya'o// 'tshams gnyis par rgya mtsho chu lha'i gzugs 'dzin pa gzhag par bya'o// gsum par pad ma chen po nyi ma'i gzugs can gzhag par bya'o// bzhi par pad ma chen po rlung gi gzugs 'dzin pa
15b1(rgyud): gzhag par bya'o// phyi'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'tshams rnams su brI hrIM gI di lha mo bzhi gzhag par byaste/ thams cad kyang g.yas na rang gi mtshan ma 'dzin pa/ g.yon pa pad ma 'dzin pa'o// sgo rnams su
15b2(rgyud): ni 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang gti mug dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtshan ma rnams gzhag par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ bud med kyi gzugs dang / sbrul gyi gzugs dang / phag gi gzugs
15b3(rgyud): dang / pad ma'i gzugs zhes bya'o// de nas gos dkar po bgos te/ gos dkar pos gdong g.yogs la pad ma chen po phyag rgya me tog dang / bcas pa bcings te zhugs la/ me tog gtor bar byas nas gang
15b4(rgyud): du babs pa de des sgrub par bya'o// des nas pad ma blangs la pad ma'i ming gis dbang skur la/ 'di skad ces brjod par bya zhing / pad ma'i 'dab ma la lta bas lci bar bya ste/ ci ltar pad ma dmar po 'di
15b5(rgyud): mtshon gyi nyes pas mi gos te// 'dam gyi nang na dag pa ltar// 'dod chags zhe sdang la sogs de bzhin// de ltar chos rnaMs/ sgom na ni// blo ldan nyon mongs bcas pa gyur kyang // 
15b6(rgyud): nyon mongs kun las rnam grol nas// myur du sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur// zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'di la gzigs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang phyug nyid thob par 'gyur te/ dade nas bcom
15b7(rgyud): ldan 'das spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ces mtshan btags so// de nas brtsams te bdag nyid kyi dngos po thams cad shin du yong su dag pa dang / mi tshugs zhing dngos grub thams cad byang chub kyi snying po
15b8(rgyud): bar du rjes myong bar 'gyur zhing / myur du sangs rgyas nyid thob par gyur te/ slob ma gzhug pa'i cho ga rgyas pa yang de bzhin no// ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor ro// sgrub pa la ni de bzhin du// ras kyi ri mo
16a1(rgyud): gnyis kyis dngos grub thams cad thob par 'gyur ro// de nas ma sgrubs kyang thams cad rjes su chags par bya ba la ni/ pad ma la lan stong rtsa zlas te sbyin par bya'o// thams cad gsad pa
16a2(rgyud): la pad ma chen po khro ba'i phyag rgyas so// thams cad rmongs par bya ba la ni// pad ma chen po phag gis so// nyan mongs pa thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba la ni/ pad ma chen po rnam par gzigs pa'i ting
16a3(rgyud): 'dzin gyi phyag rgyas so// sa thams cad kyi bdag por nying du bya ba la ni// sa la dkyil mo dkrung bcas nas bzlas brjod 'bum byas nas/ mthar mtshan thog thag zla'o// chu thams cad dbab pa la ni klu dris
16a4(rgyud): nas de'i steng du 'dug ste bzlas brjod pa'o// thams cad snang bar bya ba la ni// mun par nyi ma'i 'od kyis so// rlung thams cad dgag pa dang // gzhug pa dang / bcing ba dang / dbang du bya ba la ni// 
16a5(rgyud): pad ma chen po rlung gi mchog gis so// bde ba chen po rdo rje do// yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ nyon mongs pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i rtag pa'i
16a6(rgyud): rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i thas cad kyi khams gsum bdag po yang / de bzhin gshegs pa
16a7(rgyud): thams cad kyis dbang skur ba las byung ba ye shes kyi snying po zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad de// dbang skur ba'i phyin pa ni khams gsum thams cad kyi rgyal srid thob par 'gyur ro// 
16a8(rgyud): nor sbyin pa ni re ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// chos sbyin pa ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid thob par 'gyur ro// zang zing sbyin pa ni lus dang ngag dang / sems kyi bde ba thams cad thob par
16b1(rgyud): 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po na mkha'i snying po bzhin du rab du 'dzum dang bcas te/ rang gi mgo la rdo rje rin po che dbang bskur ba'i phreng ba 'ching zhing / don nyid rgya cher
16b2(rgyud): ston te/ dbang bskur ba thams cad kyi dam tshig rin po che zhes bya ba'i snying po 'dadi gsungs so// traMHde nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis bcom ldan 'das kyis rin po che de las thams cad dbang skur ba la spogs
16b3(rgyud): ba yo byad dang sder thams cad phyung ste/ bcom ldan 'das dang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyis byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs nyid kyis bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying po dbang skur
16b4(rgyud): ba thams cad kyi rin po che rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/ nor bu rin po che'i dam tshig ces bya ba dkyil 'khor 'di gsung so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ni dang po'i dkyil
16b5(rgyud): 'khor gyi tshul du byas pa'i nang du rin po che'i zur rgyad rin po che'i ka ba brgyad la gnas pa'i dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'i tshul los rin po che'i lkugs mas yongasu skor ba'i rdo rje rin po che'i rab
16b6(rgyud): mchog dang / me tog gi phreng ba dang / ba dan dang / gdugs dang / rnga yab kyi nye bar mdzes pa bri bar bya'o// de'i dbusu bcom ldan 'das rta'i khri la bzhugs pa dbang skur ba'i phreng ba rang nyid 'ching ba mdzad cing
16b7(rgyud): nal rnam par brnyed pa/ ma dgad kyi mdog can gzhag par bya'o// de'i mdun du byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang sbyar ba zhes bya ba rdo rje rin po che'i gcod pan 'dzin pa gzhag par bya'o// 
16b8(rgyud): g.yas su rin po che chen po nor sbyin dpag gi gter 'dzin pa gzhag go// rgya bo du chos chen po'i grags pam 'dzin pa gzhag par bya'o// g.yon du rin po che chen po'i myong ba zas dang skom thams cad 'anganam
17a1(rgyud): gzhag par bya'oka 'tshams rnams su mchod pa'i lha mo rnams rin po che'i gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / rnga dang srog shing rnams gzhag par bya'o// phyi rol gyi 'tshams bum pa gang ba rnams so// sgo
17a2(rgyud): rnams su ni dbang skur ba la sogs pa'i mtshan sa rnams gzhag par bya'o// phyi rol du ni gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang bla re rnams kyis khyab par bya'o// de nas de bzhin du rdo rje rin po che'i phyag rgya 'dzin pa
17a3(rgyud): zhugs nas/ de nas brtsams te nor thams cad 'grub pa la sogs pa'i dngos grub thams cad thob par 'gyuraro// de nas zhugs kyang dbang skur ba'i phreng bcings te/ rin po che blangs nas/ rin po che'i ming gi dbang skur
17a4(rgyud): ba la sbyin pa thams cad phul nas slar byung ba ltar ro// slob ma ga zhug pa'i cho ga rgyas pa yang de bzhin no// rdo rje rin po che'i dkyil 'khor ro// sgrub pa dang dngos grub rnams kyang de bzhin no// de
17a5(rgyud): nas ma sgrubs par yang dbang skur ba thams cad thob pa la ni/ rin po che'i dbang skur pa'i phreng bas so// bsam pa thams cad yongasu rdzogs pa ni nyin re zhing nyi ma 'char kar bzlas brjod dpag tu
17a6(rgyud): med pa byas pas so// chos thams cad kyi don shes pa la dri ma med pa'i na mkha' la la zhing zlas brjod bya'o// zas dang skom thams cad la sogs pa dang / ro thams cad thob par bya ba la ni/ na mkha' la yid
17a7(rgyud): 'dod pa bzhin du nyin re bzhing / bcom ldan 'das kyis bzlas brjod stong byas paso// shin du mthon po thob par bya ba la ni/ gdugs bzung nas bzlas brjod 'bum bya'o// rnam par rgyal ba chen po thob
17a8(rgyud): pa la ni/ rin chen rgyal mtshan mchog gis so// grags pa dang / snyan pa chen po dang / ming thob par bya ba la ni/ nyin re zhing kha zas thams cad du ltas nas/ bzlas brjod bya'o// bdag po chen po
17b1(rgyud): thob pani rin po che srog gis so// bde bachen po don men yod pa'i dam cig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ dbang skur pa thams cad rin pe che dang tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po rdzogs s+ho/ 
17b2(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur 'dzin pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa rtag pa'i yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya byin gyis brlab pa rdo
17b3(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi sku'i phyag rgya yongasasu 'dzin pa ni lus de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad nyid du 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thad
17b4(rgyud): kyi gsung gi phyag rgya yongs su 'dzin pa ni chos thams cad thob par 'gyu ro/ nga de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya yongs su 'dzin pa ni ting nge 'dzin thams cad yongs su thob par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs
17b5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i phyag rgya yongs su 'dzin pa ni/ lus dang / ngag dang / sems thams cad kyi thugs rdo rjer rdo rje'i dngos grub/ dam pa thob par 'gyur ro// su la la shes rab kyi pha rol tu
17b6(rgyud): phyin pa'i tshul 'di nyan pa dang 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / lung 'bog pa dang / sgom pa dang / des dngos grub thams cad dang phun sum tshogs pa thams cad dang / shes pa thams cad dang /

17b8(rgyud): bya bar 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje khu chu dam tshig ca po'o// rdo rje'i phyag rgya yong su 'dzin pas don gnas pa 'di myer ston te/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing rdo rje
18a1(rgyud): sra ba'i phyag rgya thams cad kyi dngos grub kyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i snying po 'di gsungs so// a/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la sogs pa sems
18a2(rgyud): can thams cad/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' phyag rgya thams cad kyis rdo rje sems dpa' nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la sogs pa dngos grub kyi mchog gi rgyus rgyas gdab po// bcom
18a3(rgyud): ldan 'das rdo rje khu tshur gyi yang sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje thams cad las phyag rgya chen po la sdog pa phyag rgya thams cad la ni dam tshig gi sems dpa' phyung nas/ dang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshul
18a4(rgyud): gyis zhugs par gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpo'i rdo rje khur de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par
18a5(rgyud): zhugs nas/ phyag rgya thams cad kyi rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di gsungaso// phyi'i dkyil 'khor/ dang po'i sbyor ba'i bris la/ nang du rdo rje thig gi 'khor lo
18a6(rgyud): bri'o// de bzhin du de'i dbus su/ dkyil 'khor brgyad pa thig btab la dbus su/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje khu tshur phyag rgya bcings la/ zhal rnam por gnad pa gzhag par bya'o// de'i mdun du rdo rje
18a7(rgyud): sku mchog ces bya ba rdo rje'i bsems pa 'dzin pa'o// g.ya su rdo rje ljags zhes bya ba rdo rje'i lce'i mchog 'dzin pa'o// rgyab tu ting nge 'dzin rdo rje zhes bya ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'o// g.yon du rdo rje rdo rje zhes bya ba bsnyem pa 'dzin/ 
18a8(rgyud): pa'o// shar lho 'tsham su phyag rgya'i khu tshur zhes bya ba dang gnyis la ni nor gyi khu tshur zhes bya ba dang / gsum pa la ni chos kyi khu tshur zhes bya ba dang / bzhi pa la ni las kyi khu tshur zhes bya ba rang gi phyag/ 
18b1(rgyud): rgya ba phyag mtshan yang 'dzin par bya'o// sgo rnams su ni de rje ba skems ma la sogs pa'i phyag rgya rnams bri bar bya'o// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya yongasu bzung ba rang nyid zhugs nas/ phyag rgyathams cad kyi slong
18b2(rgyud): dpon du 'gyur ro// de nas brtsams te dngos grub thams cad don yod pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// phyag rgya thams cad kyi ye shes dbang phyug bla na med yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu myur du mngon par rdzogs par
18b3(rgyud): 'tshang rgya bar 'gyuraro// der zhugs nas phyag rgya bcings pas bcom ldan 'das las bslab par bya zhing // rdo rje ming gis dbang skur bas dbang skur la// 'di skad ces brjod par bya'o// sku gsung thugs kyi
18b4(rgyud): rdo rje yi// gzugs brnyan lta bur sbyor ba yi// phyag rgya rgya kun zhes bya bar sgrags// dam tshig dngos grub kun ster ba'o// slob ma gzhug pa la de bzhin no// phyag rgya thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor
18b5(rgyud): bsgrub pa dang / dngos grub thams cad kyang de bzhin no// de nas ma bsgrubs pa'i las rnams kyang de bzhin no// phyag rgya thams cad bcing ba sgrub pa la ni snying khar rdo rje khu tshur gyis so// rlu phyag rgya
18b6(rgyud): thams cad sgrub pa la ni// rje rje chen po'i khu tshur gyis so// dam tshig thams cad sgrub pa la ni// rdo rje 'dod pa'i khu tshur gyis so// sems can thams cad rjes su chags par bya ba la ni// rdo rje chags po nan ma
18b7(rgyud): khu tshur gyis so// thams cad dbang du bya ba la ni// rdo rje bshad pa'i khu tshur gyiso// thams cad bcing ba la ni rdo rje bsdums pa'i khu tshur chen pos so// thams cad bsdams pa la ni// rdo rje lu gu rgyud kyi lu
18b8(rgyud): tshur gyiso// thams cad lhug par bya ba la ni/ rdo rje nal zhal gyi khu tshur gyis so// thams cad btsir ba la ni// rdo rje sngams pa'i khu tshur gyis so// thams cad bsad pa la ni// rdo rje khro bo'i khu tshur
19a1(rgyud): gyis so// thams cad bza' ba ni gnod sbyin gyi khur tshur gyis so// thams cad gzhig pa ni rdo rje nges par btsir ba'i khu tshur gyis so// thams cad dral ba la ni// rdo rje dril bu'i khu
19a2(rgyud): tshur gyis so// thams cad dbab pa la nI/ rdo rje 'bebs pa'i khu tshur gyis so// thams cad gar byed ga zhug pa la ni/ rdo rje gar gi khu tshur gyis so// thams cad sbyar gzhug pa ni rdo rje gsung gi khu
19a3(rgyud): chur gyes so// thams cad rengs par byed pa la ni// rdo rje dmigs pa'i khu tshur byis so// gzhan gyi dpung thams cad lkug pa dang / phye bor bya ba la ni rdo rje chen po phyi'o// khu tshu rigs so// phyag rgya thang
19a4(rgyud): dkrol ba la ni/ rdo rje thar pa'i khu tshur gyis so// rdo rje nas 'gro ma thams cad phyag rgyas gzhig pa la ni/ rdo rje hUM mdzad kyi rdo rje khu tshur gris so// bdug pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya dbye ba la ni tsA
19a5(rgyud): mdzad kyi rdo rje khu tshur gyiso// phyag rgya thams cad bcings pa la ni rdo rje khu tshur gyis// thams cad rgyas gdab pa la ni/ rdo rje ma mo'i khu tshuragyiso// thams cad bye mar bya ba la ni rdo rje bzang po'i
19a6(rgyud): khu tshur gyi so// thams cad rnam par gzhig par bya ba la ni/ rdo rje bdug pa'i khu tshur gyis so// thams cad gzhig pa dang / thams cad gzhom pa'i la nI/ dbang po'i dzi rje khu tshur gyis so// chu'i nang du
19a7(rgyud): gnas shing chags pa la ni/ rdo rje gnon po'i khu tshur gyis/ gzugs mang por smon pa la ni sna tshogs rdo rje khu tshur gyis so/ mi snang ba'i dngos gru ba la ni/ mi snang ba'i rdo rje khu tshur gyiso// rgyung dang
19a8(rgyud): rgyu ba'i gnas dngos po rnams 'byung ba la ni/ rdo rje na mkha'i khu tshur gyiso// na mkha' la 'gro ba'i dngos grub la ni rdo rje khu tshur gyis so// reg pa 'dzin pa'i dngos grub la ni/ rdo rje ral gyi khu tshur gyis so// 
19b1(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mchad pa'i dngos grub la na/ rdo rje las kyi khu tshur gis so/ thams cad mkhyen pa grub pa la ni/ rdo rje ye shes kyi khu tshur gyis so// nor thams cad kyi dngos grub la ni
19b2(rgyud): rdo rje nor gyi khu tshur gyis so// phyag rgya thams cad bdag nyid la ni/ rdo rje phyag rgya'i khu tshur gyis so// las thams cad kyi dngos grub la ni/ rdo rje thams cad kyi khu tshur gyis so// dkyil 'khor tha~Md grub pa/ 
19b3(rgyud): la ni/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i khu tshur gyis so// rang nyid 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar gyi dngos grub rnams ston pa la ni/ rdo rje mchog gi khu tshur gyis so// rdo rje 'dzin pa la ni rdo rje snyems pa
19b4(rgyud): khu tshur gyis so// sangs rgyas nyid la ni de bzhin gshegs pa/ thams cad kyi khu tshur gyis so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yong ba'i dam tshig gi cog/ pa'i rgyal po las/ phyag rgya thams cad kyi khru
19b5(rgyud): chur gyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das chos tha~Md spros pa med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pas yang 'a
19b6(rgyud): lo lngar yi ge bskor po zhes bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// ngo bo nyid med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad stong pa'o// mtshan ma med pa'i tshul gyis// chos thams cad mtshan ma
19b7(rgyud): med pa'o// smon pa med pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad smon pa med pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa yongs su dag pas chos tha~Md rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'o// de nas macom ldan 'das la ma dpal gzhonas
19b8(rgyud): gyur pas don 'di nyid rgya cher ston to// bzhin 'dzum pa'i bzhin du ral gyi nges de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md la 'debs shing shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i snying po 'di gsungaso// a/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsa gyis
20a1(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'dus par mdzad nas/ dang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi nal gyis bzhugs so// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med par spros pa med pa'i
20a2(rgyud): ral gri zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/ 'khor lo ltar skor ba'i yi ge zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'di gsung so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ci lta ba'i nang du 'khor lo bris la/ a la sogs pa'i yi ge'i phreng ba/ 
20a3(rgyud): gi rim bzhin du bya bar bya'o// de nas dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'i tshul gis thig btab pa de'i lte ba la bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i cha lugs 'chang zhing 'dzum pa dang bcas pa/ na mkha'i bcad phyag bzhi dang
20a4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyil 'debs par gzhag par bya'o// de'i 'dun la sogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams/ gzhag par bya'o// phyi'i 'jams rnams/ 'tshams ma bani
20a5(rgyud): gzhag pa raM bya'o// 'di lta ste/ ral gri dang / mdung dang lhung zed dang glegs bam rnamaso// de nas ral gri dang glegs bam gyi phyag rgya de bzhin du chos kyi slob dpon du byin gyis brlob po// de nas
20a6(rgyud): ral gri blangs te ral gri ming gi dbang skur bas dbang skur la/ 'di skad ces chos 'di bshad par bya ste/ ral gri 'di ni rtag zung la// shes rab tshul 'di dka' smra zhing // nam mkha' sangs rgyas sbyor ba yi/ 
20a7(rgyud): 'debs na sangs rgyas myur du 'gyur// sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung phyir dang // sems can mang po bsrung bya'i phyir// 'dir bsad sdig par mi 'gyur zhing // bsod nams ngag kyang thob par 'gyur// slob ma
20a8(rgyud): rnams la'ang de bzhin du/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa yong su rdzogs pa'i dngos grub rnams kyis/ myur du blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'chang rgya bar 'gyuraro// chos kyi
20b1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor lo// bsgrub pa'ang de bzhin no// ma bsgrubs par yang de bzhin du las rnams 'grub par 'gyur ba ni/ song pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin thob pa lA ni/ thams cad mkha' 'gro bsgoms pas so// 
20b2(rgyud): mtshan ma med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa la ni// mtshan ma dang bral ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa la ni bsgoms paso// smon pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa la ni/ smyon pa med pa bsgoms paso// rang bzhin gyis
20b3(rgyud): 'od gsal ba chos kyi ye shes thob pa la ni// shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa bsgoms pas so// nyon mongs pa thams cad thog cod pa ni/ chos sgoms pas so// yi ge thams cad kyi nges pa'i tshig gi
20b4(rgyud): ye shes la ni/ spros pa med pa'i ye shes bsgoms paso// gnas thams cad du yi ge chos kyi bam thob pa la ni/ a la sogs pa'i yi ge'i ngo bo nyid bsgoms paso// de bzhin gshegs pa
20b5(rgyud): thams cad byang chub thob pa la ni/ rdo rje ral gri'i phyag rgyas so// bde ba chen po don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ 'khor lo chen po ltar yi ge skor ba'i dam tshig ces
20b6(rgyud): bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i nang du 'dus pa'i de bzhin gshegs
20b7(rgyud): bas yang 'khor lo chen po la 'jug po zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// rdo rje mnyam nyid lo 'jug pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par 'gyuro
20b8(rgyud): don gyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni/ 'khor lo thams cad la yang 'jug par 'gyuraro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba nyid kyi don 'di rgya cher snyan cing bzhin/ 
21a1(rgyud): rab tu 'dzum nas/ rdo rje 'khor lo thams cad la 'jug pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i snying po 'di gsungs so// hUM de nas 'di gsums pa tsam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying
21a2(rgyud): po can khams gsum du rtogs pa'i sems can thams cad dkyil 'khor du zhugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi dam tshig sems dpa' rnams nges par
21a3(rgyud): byung nas/ dkyil 'khor gyi tshul gyi ji lta ba bzhin du zhug so/ de nas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje khro bo 'khor lo thams cad la rab tu 'jug pa'i phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ti nge 'dzin
21a4(rgyud): la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil 'khor thams cad la 'jug pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungaso/ phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du byas te/ nang gi dkyil 'kho
21a5(rgyud): du rdo rje 'khor lo bris la/ dbus su rdo rje 'khor lo bskor ba gzhag par bya'o// phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' tha~Md du dkyil 'khor dang po'i tshul du gzhag par bya'o// phyi'i dkyil 'am
21a6(rgyud): gyi 'tshams rnam su rnga rigs kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi bri bar bya'o// sgo rnamasu mtshan ma rnams gzhag par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sku dang rdo rje khro bo'i sku dang / spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi sku dang / 
21a7(rgyud): nim pa'i snying po'i skun maso// de nas 'khor me'i phyag rgyas ji lta ba bzhin du dkyil 'khor thams cad du sangs rgyas nyid dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid du 'grub par 'gyuraro// de nas 'khor lo blangs la/ 'a kho lo'i mang
21a8(rgyud): gi dbang skur ba blangs pa bya zhing / gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor bzhi'i thig btab pa'i rigs rnams la/ 'jug par bya'o// slob ma gzhug pa yang de bzhin no// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'kho'o// sgrub pa yang
21b1(rgyud): de bzhin mo/ ma bsgrubs par yang dkyil 'khor thams cad du 'jug pa la dri rdo rdo 'khor lo so// rang gi khar bcug la gzhag par bya'o// dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni/ 'khor lo chen thos so// 
21b2(rgyud): de bzhin du phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor 'jug pa la ni/ de bzhin gshegs thams cad kyi nga 'khor lo'i phyag rgyas so// de bzhin du dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni/ dam tshig
21b3(rgyud): phyag rgyas/ las kyi dkyil 'khor du ni zhugs pa la ni/ rdo rje thams cad kyi 'khor los so// de bzhin du rjesu chags pa dang / dbang du bya ba dang / don thob pa dang / rgyus gdab pa dang / bcad pa dang / 
21b4(rgyud): 'jug pa dang / mchod pa dang / gdug pa 'dul ba'i las rnams la nisems dpa' chen po rgyad kyi phyag g.yon na 'khor lo dang bcas phra rnams kyiso// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog
21b5(rgyud): pa'i rgyal po las dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rdo rje dam tshig ces brtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa tha~Md
21b6(rgyud): kyi cho ga rgyas pa snod kyi mchod pa thams cad kyi mchog ces bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// byang chub tu sems bskyed pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// sen
21b7(rgyud): gyi khams thams cad yongasu skyob pa nyid ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// dam pa'i chos yongasu 'dzin pa na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi la mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// shes
21b8(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yig 'dri ba las dang / yi ge 'drir gzhug pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang / brjod pa dang / ston pa dang / nyan pa dang / sos pa dang / skom pa dang / brjod par byed pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md
22a1(rgyud): mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnamakha' mdzod don de nyid rgya chen son/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing las thams cad don yod pa'i dam tshig ces
22a2(rgyud): bya ba'i snying po 'di gsungaso// de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis na mkha'i khams las mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas pa na mkha'i khams ma lus ma spros par gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das na mkha'
22a3(rgyud): mdzod kyi byang chub sems dpa'i tshul gyis dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul du zhugs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' na mkha' mdzod mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas par byin gyis brlob pa zhes bya
22a4(rgyud): bya'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje'imachod pa'i mchog don yod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba 'di gsungaso/ 1phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba de bzhin du nang gi rin po che ka brgyad/ 
22a5(rgyud): byas pa dbus su bcom ldan 'das mtshon sna tshogs 'dzin pa/ zhal 'dzum pa sku dang yan lag zla ba'i mdog la sogs pa'i ngag lnga'i mdog can gzhag par bya'o// de'i thang du dam tshig sas
22a6(rgyud): dpa' rnams gzhag par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ phyag na rdo rje dang / 'jig rten dbang phyug la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' brgyad po byang chub kyi sems dang ting 'dzin dang / dbang skur ba dang / phyag rgya
22a7(rgyud): yongasu 'dzin pa dang / skyong pa nyid smra ba dang / dkyil 'khor bri ba dang / mchod pa thams cad dang / sems can thams cad yongasu skyob pa ni/ bla na med pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa phyag na 'dzin pa'i tshul gyis
22a8(rgyud): ji lta ba bzhin du gzhag go// phye'i mtshams ni me tog la sogs pa rnams dang / sgo rnams dbyig pa dang / gser dang mu tig dang / rin po che dang / mtshan ma bzhi gzhag por bya'o// de nas de bzhin du rdo rje
22b1(rgyud): thams cad kyi mchod pa thams cad thob par 'gyur ro// zhugs nas sna tshogs rdo rje blangs la// sna tshogs rdo rje'i ming gi dbang skur nas// mchod pa rnam pa bzhi bya ste/ 'di lta ste lus kyi las thaMd dang / 
22b2(rgyud): phyag bya ba dang / ngag dang yid dang / sems kyi chos dbyings la sogs pas mchod cho ga rgyas pa thams cad kyis mchod par bya zhing rdo rje dang / phyag rgya mchod pas gcig tu byas pa'o// slob ma rnams
22b3(rgyud): gzhug pa'i las kyang de bzhin no/ las kyi dkyil 'khor ro// de nas sgrub pa dngos grub dag kyang de bzhin no// de nas ma bsgrubs par yang byang chub kyi sems kyi mchod pa la ni/ rang gi snying khar rdo rje sgom
22b4(rgyud): bso// ting 'dzin gyis mchod pa la ni thams cad dag pas sgos dpos so// dbang skur ba'i mchod pa la ni rdo rje dbang skur ba sna tshogs so// phyag rgya'i mchod pa la ni sna tshogs rdo rje thams cad kyis so// 
22b5(rgyud): stong pa nyid kyi mched pa la ni/ a la sogs pa'i yi ge'i lung snyan paso// dkyil 'khor gyi mchod pa la ni/ rdo rje 'khor lo/ sna tshogs kyiso// mchod pa thams cad la ni sna tshogs rdo rjes// 
22b6(rgyud): bdug pa 'dul bas mchod pa la ni khro bos so// me tog la sogs pa dor ba la ni bzlas pas so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ sna tshogs rdo rje don yod pa'i dam
22b7(rgyud): tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldanas de bzhin gshegs pa gdug pa thams cad 'dul nus pas/ yang ye shes kyi khu tshur yongs 'dzin pas sems
22b8(rgyud): can thams cad 'dul ba ye shes kyi snying po zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// sems can mnyam pa nyid pas khro ba mnyam nyid do// sems can thaMd 'dul ba nyid pas khro ba 'dul
23a1(rgyud): nyid do// sems can thams cad chos nyid pas the bcos nyid do// sems can thams cang rdo rje nyid pas khro rdo rje nyid // ngo ci'i phyir nem/ 'di ltar sems can thams cang 'dus pa 'i byang chub bo// denas
23a2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' bdud kyi stobs rab tu 'joms pa'i don de nyid rgya cher ston te/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing rdo rje mche ba'i phyag rgya dang / rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi gzugs kyi rdo rje khro bo'i gad mo zhes bya ba'i snying po 'di smras
23a3(rgyud): hUM/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis bdug pa can thams cad 'dul ba'i sems dpa' bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi thugs las phyung ste/ drang po dkyil 'khor gyi tshul du bzhug so// de nas byang chub sems rba
23a4(rgyud): rdo rje gnod sbyin thams cad kyis 'dul ba khro bo'i rdo rje zhes bya pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ bdug pa thams cad 'dul zhing byin gyis brlab pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi dkyil
23a5(rgyud): 'khor gsungs so// phyi yi dkyil 'khor tshul du ni// phyi yi dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// de yi nang rim nyid du ni// dkyil 'khor bze po grub bzhi pa// sgo bzhi pa la thig bzhir ldan// tshon sna lnga ni rnam
23a6(rgyud): par bris// ka ba brgyad kyi mdun gnas par// 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor yang dag ldan// de yi dbus su ci rigs par// rdo rje gnod sbyin gzhag bya ste// rdo rje metsha ma brtsegs pa dang / 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrigs
23a7(rgyud): pa'i 'od// 'jigs byed kha dog sngo ba dang // ha ha zhes grand gsal ba'i zhal// de yi kun du gnod sbyin ni// shin du 'jigs pa gzhag par bya// de nyid dang po la stsogs mchog phyag na rdo rje la srog
23a8(rgyud): mtshan// phyi yi dkyil 'khor 'tshams rnams/ mche ba'i phyag rgya bri bar bya// sgo'i gonas ni thams cad du// rdo rje'i mtshan ma gzhag par bya// de nas 'jug pa la sogs 'byung ste/ 
23b1(rgyud): mche ba'i phyag rgya dang / ha ha zhes gzhad pa dang bcas pa dang / bzhugs nas bdug pa thams cad 'dul nus shing myur du rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid thob par 'gyur ro// de nas zhugs nas rdo rje mche ba blangs nas
23b2(rgyud): rdo rje mi nga gi dbang skur bas dbang skur te/ rdo rje rdo rje gnod sbyin nyid la bsnun no// de nas rdo rje gnod sbyin gyi zhal nas// ha ha zhes bya ba'i sgra 'byung bar 'gyuro// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
23b3(rgyud): gzhin gshegs pa thams cad bsrung ba po gnod sbyin gyi bdag po chen po phyag na rdo rje zlum por bdag grub pa yin no// zhes shes par bya'o// de nas phyag rgya thams cad bcing bar bya zhing sgrub par bya'o// de
23b4(rgyud): nas mchod la de bzhin du yang dag par tshim par byas nas/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul lan cig brjod la slar blang bar bya'o// de bzhin du phyag rgya bcing ba la sogs pa'i cho ga rgyas pa ni dang po/ 
23b5(rgyud): la sogs dkyil 'khor thams cad du bya'o// phyag na rdo rje'i/ dkyil 'khor ro// sgrub pa dang dngos grub kyang de bzhin no// ma// bsgrubs par yang dang po ji lta ba bzhin no// bdug pa thams cad
23b6(rgyud): 'dul ba la ni/ rdo rje mche ba'i phyag rgyaso// sems can thams cad 'dul ba la ni/ khro bos ha ha zhes rgod cing 'dul bas so// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba las
23b7(rgyud): ltung bar bya ba la ni chos gos snam sbyar gyi sbyin sreg gis so// dbang skur ba thams cad dbrog pa la ni// khams thams cad kyi phye me'i sbyin sreg gis so// thams cad rgyas btab pa la ni/ 
24a1(rgyud): byaH shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i rdul 'di bshad do// chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid bas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i mnyam pa nyid do// chos thams cad don nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin don nyid do// thams cad chos
24a2(rgyud): cing bas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa chos nyid do// thams cad/ de las mnyam pa nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa mnyam pa nyid du rig par bya'o// de nas phyag na bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de
24a3(rgyud): bzhi gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi don yod pa'i das nig gi dkyil 'khor byin gyis brjod ba'i zhes skye po'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ don mong pa thams cad kyi sa
24a4(rgyud): cig ces bya ba'i snying po 'di smras// hUM de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la sogs pa dkyil 'khor thams cad thugs las byung ste/ dam tshig gi de kho na nyid rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
24a5(rgyud): chen po'i ngor zhugs par gyur to// de nas phyag na rdo rjes bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la nges par btud nas/ dam tshig chen po'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor chen po bris la/ dkyil
24a6(rgyud): 'khor gyi gnas brgyad du rdo rje khas gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i la sogs pa'i dkyil 'khor gzhag go/ de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje dam tshig thams can kyi rdo rje byin gyis brlob pa zhes bya ba'i
24b1(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin la sems par zhugs nas/ dam tshig thams cad kyi rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul du phyi'i dkyil 'khor bris la/ de'i dbus su rdo rje'i 'khor le bris nas
24b2(rgyud): 'khor lo'i gnas rnams su dkyil 'khor chen po la sogs pa bri bar bya'o// thams cad kyang dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'i thig btab rtsipa sems dpa' chen po gnag par bya'o// phyi'i dkyil
24b3(rgyud): 'khor du phyi rol gyi rdo rje'i rigs ji ltar rjes su 'thun par bri bar bya'o// sgo rnams su rigs bzhi'i mtshan ma rnams gzhag par bya'o// de nas dam tshig chen po'i de kho na nyid kyi rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul
24b4(rgyud): gyis chog thams cad rgyas par bya'o// dam tshig chen po'i rngo rje'i de kho na nyid kyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ bde ba thams cad kyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i
24b5(rgyud): rgyal po chen po rdzogs s+ho// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad/ rnam par snang mdzad kyis/ yang sems can thams cad byin gyis rlong
24b6(rgyud): pazhes bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun du bzang po thams cad kyi rang bzhin yin pas/ sems can thams cad ni de bzhin
24b7(rgyud): gshegs pa'i snying po can no// thams cad rdo rje snying pos dbang skur ba nyid pas/ sems can thams ca ni rdo rje'i snying po can no// ngag thams cad rab tu byung ba se sems rgyan thams cad ni chos kyi
24b8(rgyud): snying po can no// sems can thams cad kyi byang byed pa la sbyor bas/ sems can thams cad kyilas ni stong po cad do/ denas phyi rol gyi ro rdo'i rigs rnams kyis tsaco'o sa phung nas
25a1(rgyud): nyid kyi don rgya cher ston te/ snying po phul te/ de nas rdo rje dbang phyug chen pos de kho na nyid snying po 'di phul lo// triHde nas dkyil 'khor bshad par bya ste/ kun nas zlum pa'i thig
25a2(rgyud): gsum pa// dkyil 'khor chen po sgo bzhi pa// 'tshams rnamasu mdung rtse gsum bya'o// de'i dbus su dbang phyug chen po bri bar bya'o// de'i logs thams cad du tshogs bdag brgyad po bri bar bya'o// 'di lta ste/ 
25a3(rgyud): nag po chen po dang / dga' byed dbang phyug chen po dang / gang gi dbang phyug rnams ni phyogs su'o// 'tshams rnamasu ni thod pa bzang po dang // gtum pa'i dbang phyug dang / lag na kha traM kha dang / ba la rna'i dbang //

25a5(rgyud): phyi rol du ni 'byung po rnams dang / yid btags rnams bri ba bya'o// de nas slob dpon thal ba gtsang mas lus skus shing gos gtsang ma bgos te/ mdung rtse gsum gyi mtshan ma gzhug
25a6(rgyud): par bya'o// zhugs nas kyang snying po bzlas par bya'o// de nas slob ma de bzhin du bcug la lag par mdung rtse gsum pa byin nas chos bshang bar bya'o// sems cad kun la phan phyir dang // bstan pa thams cad

25b1(rgyud): rnyed bro bani pa'i mdu sung gis padun su skyed do'o/ denam pa mo 'thams cad bcom ldan 'das 'byug la la te/ da ngos zin gcig tu mas cang dashug pa dang / 'azhug pa das gsang pa dang / sgrub pa'i

25b3(rgyud): phyogs dang phyogs 'tshams su drag po'i ma mo brgyad bri bar byo ste/ 'di lta ste/ drag mo dang / tshangs pa mo dang / khyab 'jug mo dang / gzhon nu mo dang / nag mo dang nag me chen mo dang / sho za mo dang / srin

25b7(rgyud): ba'i pho nya phyag rgyas zhugs la snying po zla bar bya'o// de nas dkyil 'khor gyi dbus nas su byo chen po thos par 'gyur ro// de nas ngaslob dpon ma rtogs pa gzhan thams ji ltar 'ongs pa bzhugs par 'gyur
25b8(rgyud): ni/ thos par 'gyur te/ bdug pa'i dam tshig ni ma rtogs so// de nas slob ma me tog thogs pas/ ras kyi mig bka' la/ nag pa'i phyag rgya
26a1(rgyud): bcug ste/ rna bar dam tshig chen po b+h+yo zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro// de nas sgrag nas metog der ro// de nas gang du ltung ba de lhag par bsgrub par bya'o// gal te byung bar ma gyur na sang dor du bzhug/

26a7(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad ces bya ba'i phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor ro// de nas spring rtsi bad la sogs pa ming po gsum gyis bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal te/ mgrin gcig tu rang gi snying po kho na'i snying po'i dibul la/

29a1(rgyud): 'dzin pa chen po dam pa de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur ro// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig dpal mchog dang po las/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bde ba chen po rdo rje gsang ba'i

29a3(rgyud): gi dngos grub cho ga rgyas pa'i rgyal po chen po da rang bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje gsang ba'i don yod cing / brtan pa'i cho ga rgyas btab pa'i sku gsung thugs thams cad
29a4(rgyud): kyi rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dam tshig chen po thams cad la rab tu zhugs nas/ chos nyid rtogs pa'i ye shes la rab tu zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sgo sna tshogs

29b1(rgyud): dam tshig sems dpa' thams cad dang / dbang skur ba thams cad dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ting nge 'dzin las thams mchog gyur pa/ khaMs gsum thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa/ thams cad dbang phyug byed pa po
29b2(rgyud): 'dod pa thams cad pa/ rgya che ba'i cho ga thams cad pa/ rtag pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba btab pa/ ji srid pa'i gnas pa/ de srid sems can don mchog mdzod/ sems can khams ni mtha'
29b3(rgyud): yas dang // rgyal srid srid pa 'dod pa'i phyir// srid pa'i skyon rnams 'joms phyir dang // ban pa chen po 'phel ba'i phyir// gsang ba'i rtog pa mchog gsungs pa'i rtog pa rjes su gnang ba bdag srol / di nas
29b4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas chos/ thams cad de bzhin gal lhag pa'i lta ba'i dgongs nas/ gdungs bya/ thams cad thugs rje chen po'i sna tshogs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
29b5(rgyud): la snyoms par zhugs te/ ma lus shing lus pa med par sems can gyi bsam pa thams cad yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang thams cad yongs sbyangs pa dang / phan pa dang bde ba dang dngos grub thams cad phun
29b6(rgyud): sum tshogs pa dang / ye shes dang las dang mchog gi dngos grub kyi rgyur 'gyur ba'i bar du/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid dang / rdo rje 'chang chen po thob/ mchog gi dngos grub kyi don bde ba chen po'i rdo rje dang po ste/ de bzhi
29b7(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad 'khor lo bsgyur ba nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'khor lo sku'i phreng ba'i cod pan gyis dbang bskur bas dbang bskur ba yin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen po ma lus pa luH
29b8(rgyud): pa med pa'i bde pa chen po mchog gi dngos grupa thams cad tho par bya ba'i phyir/ sems dpa'i dkyil mo dkrus bcas te sku drang por snang te/ g.yon pa skems pa'i tshul gyis mdzad nas/ g.yas pade sde gsorabs rang ni
30a1(rgyud): gzugs par dang po'i ni rje sa cog ge sbyor ba 'dzin cing bad pa chen po'i dri rje zhes bya ba thams cad kyi 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs dang rnams las byung ngo // oM mat+ma s+'u kha badz+ra swA/ 
30a2(rgyud): dzA hU~M ba~M hoHsu ra ta s+t+waM/ de nas phyung ba tsam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur bzung ba rnams slar yang byang chub chen po rtogs nas/ de rnams
30a3(rgyud): kyis gzhad pa chen po mngon par mdzad do// 'jig rten gyi khams cad g.yos pa dang bcas pas yongasu dag par 'gyur ro// khams gsum rgyas pa spros pa thams cad kyang bcom ldan 'das kyi dkyil 'khor chen po
30a4(rgyud): 'gyur ro// gang gis sems can thams cad bde ba dang yid badre/ thob par 'gyuraro// de nas rdo rje 'chang chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi don yod cing thogs pa las mngon par byang ba/ 
30a5(rgyud): rdo rje chen po phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te bde ba chen po rdo rje'i dam tshig ces bya ba gnod par mdzad nas/ de'i sku thams cad nas dngos grub thams cad dang / bde ba dang / srid/ 
30a6(rgyud): bye bA ster bu rtag tu rjes su 'brel pa can lhan cig tu spyod pa bde ba chen po'i spyod pa'i dam tshig sems dpa' rnams phyung nas phyogs thams cad du byung ste/ mdun du rdo rje gsang ba yid las byung ba gas su rdo rje
30a7(rgyud): ki ge ki li'i rgyag du 'dong pa'i rdo rje/ gson du rdo rje sgyings pa'o// mtshams rnams su mchod pa'i lha mo rnams so// phyi rol gyi kho khyer 'tshas su lha'i bu bo rnam so// sgo srung ba rnams ni rdo rje lcags dkyu dang / zhags
30a8(rgyud): pa dang / lcags smos dang / dril bu 'dzin pa'i/ khyi ma du de rje gro zungs kyi tshogs dang / po nya dang bran nam mo// denas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi su chu ba rtseste/ 
30b1(rgyud): de gzhin gshegs pa thams cad byang chub rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' rdo rje 'chang chen po la gsol ba btag te/ sems can kun la bad don du// rgyal ba chen
30b2(rgyud): po 'byung ba ste// chags bral de rnams chags ldan pa// rang gi btsun mo'ang gsol mdzad pas// de phyir bdag gis khyod la gsol// bde ba chen po rdo rje che// gsang ba'i rtog pa'i dngos grub ste// 'dul ba nyid ni
30b3(rgyud): ba shad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das don yod cing thogs pa med pa'i bka' bden pa thams cad kyi dngos grub 'dul ba rdo rje 'dod pa'i mchog ces bya ba'i rnam par gnon par mdzad nas/ rdo rje gsang ba chen
30b4(rgyud): po'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di gsungs so// de nas yang dag bshad bya ba// dkyil 'khor dam pa chen po ste/ bde ba chen po rdo rje mchog/ dam tshig dam pa'i ming can yin/ dkyil
30b5(rgyud): 'khor gnas ni 'dul byas nas/ de dbus cho ga bzhin du ni// phya/ rgya chen po mnyam gzhag nas// der ni dkyil 'khor sgrub par de/ gser zhing legs par sgril ba dang // 'dud pa dag ni med bu yi/ 
30b6(rgyud): gsung dmar pos thog btu ba nas// tshon gyi byems bri bar bya// zur bzhi pa la sgo bzhu pa sgo khyud banyis ni ma dzes pa dang / k+She ga khyer gyis ni long su bskor// mtshams su lha'i bu mos mdzes// dkyil 'khor dug
30b7(rgyud): ga mtshams rnams dang // sgo dang skyo khyud 'tshams rnams su// zla ba phyed la gnas pa yi// rdo rje rin chen 'od zer 'bar// rlung gis spyod pa'i dril bu mchog/ ba dan sna tshogs mches pa yin// me tog dra ba me tog phreng / 
30b8(rgyud): ldan pa'i phyi rol dkyis 'khor bre// de'i nang du 'khor lo ni// dkyil 'khor rgyad pa dang 'dra ba// rdo rje thig gis yongs skor ba'i// rdo rje 'khor lo yang dag bri// de dbus cho ga bzhin du ni// rdo rje sems dpa' dgod
31a1(rgyud): par bya thugasas su sa na byu jug/ 'dras pa ma sang na rjes mre/ pa 'du ba dang cwam zla ba'i 'od/ 'bar ba'i 'od zer dbar pos khyag sangs rgya phreng brnam par mdzes/ 
31a2(rgyud): sku la tshon gyis rnam par byugs// sems dpo'i dkyil mo dkrungs gis bzhugs// rdo rje snyems pa 'dzin pa'i mchog nas ma ya skyom zhes brjod nas// steng khar rnam par dgod par bya// de'i logs ni tha~Md du
31a3(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po rnams bris te// tshon nAm yang na bdul tshon gyis// go rims ji bzhin bri bar bya// mdun du sku mo dag dam na mo ni// rdo rje tshon ma lasogs pa// gsas pa dag pa'i dkar po ste// legs par 'khyung
31a4(rgyud): ba'i rdo rje can// rgyab du sku mdog ser po ste// chu srin gyis ni rgyal mtshan 'dzin// g.yon du sku mo dag sngon po ste// phyag gnyis/ snyoms pa 'dzin la sogs// mchod pa'i snod rnams 'dzin pa'o// 
31a5(rgyud): mchod pa'i lha mo bri bar bya// skyeg mo gzhad ma gru ma dang // ga ma lha'i bu mo'i tshogs// rdo rje lcags dkyu zhags dang // rdo rje ldegs sgrog dril bu rnams// sgo ni bzhi po rnams la ni// sgo srungs bzhi dag
31a6(rgyud): ge snying po 'di yin te/ ts+tsha badz+rA ta~MSh+Thas sa ki paT/ hUM badz+ra ki la~M ki sa~M b+h+rU~M/ hU~M d+ha b+har badz+ra b+han d+ha g+ha~M/ hU~M d+huSh+Ta badz+ra nI b+h+rUM/ rdo rje bran no// / de nas mchod pa'i lha po rnams kyipa ni// d+h+r-i sa d+ha ru tra~M
31a7(rgyud): makroh+l-I dz+dzas 'ang badz+ra hU~M/ hU~M dz+dza badz+ra she ri ng+ga/ denas la ma rnams kyis so hUM badz+ra sa le sa hA bar badz+ra na/ oM badz+ra ki ti/ oM ni ta bAdz+ra/ de nas sgo srungs rnams kyis ni/ badz+ra a guM shi badz+ra pra te ha ra/ 
31a8(rgyud): badzub gags mas dra ga sa 'jugs te/ de gar shA ma'i dkyil lakhor du grags pa de nyi ga ba na nyid ras kyis khyen sa pa nyid tu gyur// des byas
31b1(rgyud): rdo rje 'dzin// dkyil 'khor kun mchog byas nas su// bus pa gang dag ni skyed pa// me tog la sogs kun gyis mchod// dril bu brtags pa'i ba dran rnams// mtshams rnams su yang gzhag par byad// krugs dang / 
31b2(rgyud): bcas bum pa rnams// sgo'i phyi rol dag tu gzhag/ rdo rje dang bcas bzhin dang bcas// lcug ma yongasu zlas nas ni// dri nus gang ba'i bum pa ste// phyag na rdo rje'i mdun gzhag bya// de la 'di ltar bde ba chen po'i/ 
31b3(rgyud): dam tshig gi bdud rtsi'i chu byin gyis rlabs pa'i snying po ni// oM ma hA su pa badz+ra sa ma ya/ a bi shi ka/ dza hUM baM hoH/ lan nyi shu rtsi gcig zlas so// chu 'di rtor ba 'am 'thungs na sdug bsngal thams cad byang ba 'am/ bde
31b4(rgyud): pa thams cad rab tu 'phol bar 'gyur ba yin no// de nas rang gi dam tshig rnams kyis/ rdo rje 'chang la sogs pa sgrub par bya'o// dza hU~M ba~M hoH/ zhes pas pa dang / gzhug pa dang / bcings nas/ skad cig
31b5(rgyud): dbang du 'gyur/ phyag rgya chen po mnyam gzhag ste// de bzhin g.yas 'dzub lcags dkyur bcas// dgug pa 'di na lan// cig gis// 'grub te rab tu bzhug par bya// oM ma hA kha badz+ra swA hA/ 
31b6(rgyud): a a hi she gris khe su badz+ra gud+d+ha sa sa ya/ mA na sum rab+hA ba d+ha sa sa yA s+t+wa~M/ d+hI d+hi pa su ta sh+yo i nu rag to// su bai sho me pA la A ti toSh+Tha la ga wAn/ an ti ni dan sa rnas pa rbA bo ta/ dza dz+r-i ba~M hoH/ dran
31b7(rgyud): rtag tu bcom ldan 'das dkyil 'khor du ni rang nyid byon// dgug cing bcug ni brtan pa dang // dbang du 'gyur zhing 'grub pa yin// ched du byung ba'i rdzu 'phrul dum rnams mthong ba 'am/ yang na bcom
31b8(rgyud): ldan 'das rang nyid kyis mthong bar 'gyur/ de nas rang nyid rje 'dzin pa kun gyi slob dpon ni/ phyag rgya thams cad grub pa/ dam tshig thams cad shes pa/ las thams cad nus pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byin
32a1(rgyud): gyis rlabs pa yin no// 'jug pa'i cho ga 'di yis rdo rje slob dpon rang nyid ji skyed pa'i dris byugs shing sgoms pas/ rgyan dang cha lugs dang bcas pa'i me tog gi phreng bas lus shin tu rgyun pa/ gos
32a2(rgyud): dmar po gnyis bgos pa/ rang nyid kyis bcom ldan 'das la spyod cing rdo rje dang bcas pa'i rdo rje snrums pas rang nyid 'jug par bya'o// stong pa ni drug ldan la sogs pa'i glu yis bya'o// 'dod chags la sogs pade kun
32a3(rgyud): yid khyod ni// kun sdus bdag la bde ba gsol mdzod cig/ rdo rje sems dgongs myur du bdag ston mdzod// bdag rigs mdzad dang bde mchog mdzad la 'dud// de nas rab tu zhugs nas dgongs su gsol bar bya
32a4(rgyud): ste/ thog mtha' med pa'i sems dpa' ni// rdo rje sems dpa' ba brtse// kun du bzang po khyod len te// rdo rje bsnyems bdag khya bdag yin// sems kyi sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin// de bzhin rdo rje rdo rje 'dzin
32a5(rgyud): kun mchog dam tshig dngos grub can// rdo rje sems bdag dang 'grub mdzod// de nas bcom ldan 'das de nyid kyis rdo rje slob dpon byin rlabs gyur/ snga ma byung ba'i so so rang rig pa'i badre ba gnyi
32a6(rgyud): ga kya ste bar 'gyur ro// phra sgo dbab pa yang 'gyur ro// de nas bdag la bcom ldan 'das 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas de nyid du 'dug la ci 'dod pa'i zlas brjod bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa
32a7(rgyud): du 'dug la rang gi bsod nams kyis byin gyis rlabs kyis 'dug pa'i dengs grub thob par 'gyur ro// de nas rgyas pa te sems dpa' chen po thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de rnams kyis kyang de la dngos grub thams
32a8(rgyud): cad stsol bar mdzad do// phyag rgya thams cad kyang bdag rang nyid kyis bcings na las thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// dam tshig thams cad kyang 'di la bstan par 'gyur ro// yid kyis 'dod pa'i las rnam
32b1(rgyud): kyang byed pa yin no// bde ba dang yid bde ba thams cad nyams su myong zhing gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / mi gsod pas lo cig 'das nas/ sangs rgyas nyid la sogs pa'i mchog gi dngos grub thob pa yin no// 
32b2(rgyud): de nas sems can thams cad gzhug pa'i don rtag par bya ba yin no// rdo rje slob dpon rang nyid snga ma bzhin du lus rgyan nas/ rab tu bde ba'i rdo rje'i dam tshig phyag rgya rab tu bcug te/ de bzhin du de kho na
32b3(rgyud): nyid chen po bskul bas/ yang dag par bskul las dgug par bya ste/ 'di skad ces brjod do// srid pa'i bde ba rnam dag phyir// sngar ni srid pa la khyod dga'// 'dod pa kun gyi dngos grub che// 'gro/ 
32b4(rgyud): bkunas 'du'i sgrub par bgyi// de nas sachod pa byas la rang lhag pa'i lha gang yin pa de rnam tshig drug rgya tog dang bcas pa gzug par bya ste/ bcu kun pa rna bar / 
32b5(rgyud): smab cis brjod par bya'o// chags bral 'dul ba'i 'dzi rten ni/ chags bral ba 'di nyid kyis 'dus par 'gyur 'o// 'do tshugs chen po bang bu rjen/ rdo rje sems dpa' sas
32b6(rgyud): smin 'dod chags bral ba lta bu ste// sdug bsngal gzhan mo rang bzhin meng // de bas sems can chags bral ba/ sngar yang med ni ma byed cig/ de nas mye tog la sogs pa snying po/ 
32b7(rgyud): 'dis 'dor du gzhug go// A~M badz+ra khaM buM Sh+Ta badz+rA pA trA pra ti nAM/ den sa gang du babs pa deni de'i lha yin no// nas de khon+da nyid chen po brjod par bya'o// gang 'dod pa'i snying
32b8(rgyud): byang la sgrub du bcug la/ rang nyid lhag pa'i lha'i dbang bskur nas// de'i mtshan ma lag pa gnyis su byin te/ de'i rigs kyi ming gis/ dbang bskur ba snying po 'dis dbang bskur bar/ 
33a1(rgyud): bya'o// oM sArba ad ma mahA badz+ra d+ha ra sa mu kho b+ha wa a shad taM/ ya b+hi Shiny+tsa miHg+h+ri ha nA s+yaid ti badz+ra he/ oM mo ka sId ta s+t+wa~M// de nas phyag rgya ba cing ba byin gyis
33a2(rgyud): brlabs par bya'o// de nas ci 'dod pa'i mchod pa byas shing / byed du bcug nas/ ci 'dod pa za ba dang / btung bas slob ma rnams tshim par byas la/ phyag rgyad ngo // phyag rgya'i lan dang / 
33a3(rgyud): gAr dang / rgod pa byed du bcug te/ rang nyid kyis kyang bya'o// de nas thams cad skad nas/ brjod par bya ste/ thog mthar rgya'i 'gro ba 'di dga' bo mchog la dag lus te// sems dpa' mchog la/ 
33a4(rgyud): rdo rjer 'gyur// sgor yang gshegs par mdzad du gsol// // de nas snyim pa'i me tog dor nas/ phyung bar bya'o// dkyil 'khor yang rang nyid kyis byugs las gzhag na gzhan gyi
33a5(rgyud): la sna thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas badre ba chen po rdo rje dam tshig gi bdud rtsi'i tshul du yang bcug na tshe 'phel ba la sogs pa'i las thams cad la dgongs
33a6(rgyud): pa yin no// de nyid kyis dbang bskur ba yang / dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa dang / mchog gi dngos grub kyang thob par 'gyur ro// gal te sku bri ba'i ri mo mkhan rang rang gi phyag 'tshan
33a7(rgyud): gyi phyag rgya rnams kyis/ dkyil 'khorare bri bar bya'o// gal te de yang mi shes na/ phyag mtshan gzhag byar bya'o// phyag rgya'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das don yod pa thogs
33a8(rgyud): pa med pa myur du 'grub pa'i chog rgya che ba'i dam cig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rnam par gnang ba mdzad nas/ rdo rje 'chang chen pos 'di gsungs so// 
33b1(rgyud): bde ba chen pos rab sbubs dang // 'dod pa chen pos rnam dag phyir// rdo rje sems dpa' grub la ni// brtag par myur du bshad par bya// ji srid 'khor ba'i gnas su nin// de srid sems can gdon
33b2(rgyud): par bya// mya ngan 'dres pa byang chub sgrub// de nyid kyis ni byang chub rnams// ji srid srid pa la gnas pa// de srid sems can don nyid byed// thams cad dag pa'i cho ga can// ji ltar sems
33b3(rgyud): che mo kun skye don// dngos gru ba thams cad rab sgrub po/ de ltar sbyin sogs pha rol phyin// byang chub spyod pa snachog gri ming // de bzhin gshegs mi gdul min la// sems
33b4(rgyud): can rnams kyi don mi mdzad// 'di na dngos grub rab sgrub na// dus kun tu ni thams cad mdzad// de nas sgrib 'di// bshad bya ste// dngos grub shin tu brtag pa yin// gang
33b5(rgyud): gis srid pa 'di nyid du/ shin tu brtag pa'i dngos gru ba ts+tsha// dkyil 'khor dag tu ma zhugs kyang // dam tshig rna/ bar spangs pa 'am// bsod nams med kyang thams cad du/ 
33b6(rgyud): br-i pa 'di la myur du grub// gal te dngos grub sgrub 'dod na// brtag tu yul dang ldan gyur na// gsang ba'i mchod pas mchod nas ni// rang rang phyug rgyas bsgrub par 'byum// drug stuH/ 
33b7(rgyud): la sogs bstam pa'i g+ha/ chags pa kun kyang phyi 'dod par/ bzlas pa'i don ni ni nus pas// rdo rje sems dpa' grub par bya// 'di yis 'dod kun los dbang phyug/ tso 'dod 'gro
33b8(rgyud): mkha' la rgya// dngos grub kun gyi dbang phyug grub// rga shi med cing gtso bor 'gyur// rgyal ba kun gyi mchod byas la// rang gnyen kun gyis bsnyen bkur zhing // rdo rje 'chang chen dang 'chung
34a1(rgyud): shing don yod kun mchog spyod pa yin// bde ba chen po rdo rje grub pa'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa la sogs pa'i dngos grub thams cad rab tu ster ba rdo rje 'chang chen po byang chub sems dpa
34a2(rgyud): yin no/ ta gal te de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog gi dngos grub mngon par 'dod na de bzhin gshegs pa des/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya'i khu tshur yongs su
34a3(rgyud): 'dzin pas rAs ris la bri bar bya'o// bzhad pa dang bcas pa dngos grub thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis yongs su bskor bas/ de'i mdun du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur yongasu 'dzi
34a4(rgyud): pas rdo rje'i tshig stong phrag brgya bzlas par bya'o// 'bum rdzogs pa na mtshan phyed bdud kyi tshogs rnams 'ong bar 'gyur ro// de nas bdud thams cad kyi stobs gzhom par bcom par bya'o// de nas tho rangs
34a5(rgyud): kyi dus su de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad nyid dam/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad nyid thob par 'gyur ro// gal te rdo rje 'am chen po nyid mngon par 'dod na/ des blugs ma 'am/ gdungs ma
34a6(rgyud): 'am/ ras ri sa la sogs pa bris pa'i phyag na rdo rje'i sku'i dkyil 'khor bzhin du sngar sgrub pa la/ dza sku gzugs kyi khyad par ji ltar thob pa ltar rdo rje sems dpa' sgrub par bya'o// zla ba drug gis rdo rje 'chang chen po
34a7(rgyud): dngos grub chen po 'grub po// gal te rdo rje 'chang chen po dgug bran/ byed pa chen po'i rdo rje ljags dkyu dgag cing / ci 'dod pa smrar cang bar bya'o// b+hA ba gcig 'das nas thams cad gsol bar bya'o// gas
34a8(rgyud): rang gi phyag rgyas bdag nyid sgrub na/ rang gi lha'i phyag chen bcings te/ bsgoms pas bdag rdo rje sems dpar yin no// zhes bsgoms la grub pa yin no// de ji ltar mngon par 'dod pa'i zlas pas bdag nyid sgrub par bya'o// 
34b1(rgyud): yang dang yang du sgom zhing / zlas pa de srid bdag gis bya'o// ji srid rdo rje 'chang nyid zla ba phyed 'das nas thob par 'gyur ro// de nas 'dod pa thams cad kyi dbang phyug bsgrub par 'dod na/ de bzhin du rang yid du
34b2(rgyud): 'ong ba dang / bcas par rab tu zhugs te/ phyag rgya bcings la de srid zlas par bya'o// ji srid bdag 'dod pa kun gyi dbang phyug dang / khams gsum ma lus pa'i bdag por 'gyur ro// de nas bcom 'das rdo
34b3(rgyud): rje 'chang khams gsum ma lus pa'i 'dod pa'i don yod pa'i rgyun rang bzhin thams cad grub pa'i chos nyid kyi ye shes rnam par rol par mdzad nas/ ma sgrubs pa'i phyag phyag rgya'i las kyi rgyun rdo rje cho ga rgyas pa
34b4(rgyud): 'dra gsungs te/ ma sgrubs pa'i snying po'i las thams cad 'di lta ste/ bdag nyid srung ba'i bde ba chen po'i rdo rje gsang ba'i myug da tor gyis so// thams cad srung ba la ni ba chen po rdo rje gsad
34b5(rgyud): ba'i mdzod gsungs so// phyogs thams cad dang mtshams rje dang dkyil 'khor bcing bar bya'o// dril ni bde ba chen rdo rje gsang ba'i gtsug tor gyis so// bdud thams cad
34b6(rgyud): kyi stobs gzhom pa lA ni/ bde ba chen po'i gsang ba rdo rje mi skyod pa'i tshe 'phel bya ba la ne/ bde bo chen po rdo rje gsang ba'i bdud rtsis so// gzugs chen po phun sum tshogs pa ni/ bde bo chen po rdo rje
34b7(rgyud): gsang ba'i gzugs kyis so// gzi brjid dang / na tshod shin tu bzang po rab tu 'phel ba la ni/ bde ba chen po rdo rje gsung ba'i bcud kyis len gyis so// stobs dang mdog dang 'phel ba la ni/ bde
34b8(rgyud): ba chen po rdo rje gsang ba'i mthu yin pas so// dbang bskur ba thams cad thob pa la ni/ rdo rje gsang ba'i cod pan gyis so// nor thams cad thob pa la ni rdo rje gsang ba'i dbyibs so// rgyal srid thob
35a1(rgyud): pa la ni rdo rje gsang ba'i rgyal po'i phyag rgyas so// sa ma lus pa thob la ni gsang ba'i stsal gyis so// thams cad dbab pa dang / g.yo bar bya ba dang / gar byed du gzhung pa dang / dus gsum

37b1(rgyud): phyag rgyas so// las thams cad grub pa lnga ni rdo rje gsang ba'i mchod pas so// dngos grub thams cad la ni rdo rje gsang ba'i badra ba chen po grub pas so// phun sum tshogs pa thams cad la ni rdo rje ltung

37b3(rgyud): bu chen po'i rdo rjes so// sems dpa' chen po'i thams kyi dngos grub dam pa la ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba chen pos so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dngos grub dam pa la ni/ rdo rje gsang ba mchog gi

40a1(rgyud): ga bams pas rjong/ g.yon pas pa mas 'dzin cipa de bzhin du rdo rje snyems pas rdo rje dkyir mo dkrung gis btsugs so// des dkyil 'khor ni/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul gyis so// dkyil 'khor rnams

56b6(rgyud): thams cad 'byung bar grub pa'i tshe phyir// bskal pa dang po bcom ldan gsungs// de nas yi ge hU~M gis bzlas pa don gyi bshad pa'i rgyud ni// myur du thams cad rjes chags pas/

56b8(rgyud): bsdus nas kun tu 'jug pa ni// rdo rje thog ni brtan gyur pa// de bzhin rdo rje bsdus pa'o// de nas rdo rje sems dpa' 'byung ba shes pa'i rgyud ni/ 3/ thams cad bdag nyid sems dpa' ni/ 
57a1(rgyud): myur du thams cad la yang zhugs// de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud ni// 'dod las chags pa dga' las bad// bde las sdig pa sdig las sdug/

57a3(rgyud): rigs de nyid// de nyid rdo rje rigs chen po// de nyid pad ma rigs dag pa// de nyid nor bu'i rigs mchog bshad// de nas mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud ni// rang sems so sor rtogs

57a6(rgyud): portog pa thams cad grub pa shes pa'i rgyud ni// rtog pa kun las grub bya gang // rgyu ba dang ni mi rgyu yin// rang gi lha'i rnal 'byor gyis// de dag thams cad grub par bya//

57b1(rgyud): bsngags dang rig pa gang+gA// byazlas pa don du sems dpa' che// bdag nyid ngas se sgrub bya ba// de nas dngos grub shes pa'i rgyud ni// rdo rje sems dpa'i drongos grub che// de bzhi/

58a1(rgyud): 'gyur/ de nas sdig pa chen po byed pa'ang shes pa'i rgyud ni// dkyil 'khor la ni ma zhugs kyang // tshul khrims 'chal ba la sogs pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs kyis ni/

181a8(rgyud): kha gang zhe na/ sems dpa' kun gyis bdag ces na/ bdag nyid la yang gnaso zhes/ byin gyis brlabs nas sems dpa' bdag yin zhes nga rgyal bsgom par bya// de nyid bcom ldan 'das sems dpa' ste/ rdo rje/ 
181b1(rgyud): sems dpar 'am rgyal ba yin/ rang sems so sor rtog pa ni/ rang sangs rgyas byang chub de nyid yin// de nyid phyag na rdo rje ste/ rdo rje 'dzin pa tshul gis so// 'jig dbang po na mkha' snying / de ltar gzhan yang de nyid do//

181b5(rgyud): khyad kyi gsang ba dang ting nge 'dzin ces bya'o// de la sems kye can gyi don gyi phyir gsangs brjod pa dang / smra ba ni snying po rjod pa ste/ snying po brjod pas na gzugs bstan sbyor ba 'di dag/
